PartialRMatrixPresentation[\[CapitalGamma]_, n_, V_, W_, \[Beta]_, 
    \[Lambda]_] := PartialRMatrixPresentation[\[CapitalGamma], n, V, W, 
     \[Beta], \[Lambda]] = MatrixPresentation[\[CapitalGamma]][
      PartialRMatrix[\[CapitalGamma]][n]][V \[CircleTimes] W, \[Beta], 
     \[Lambda]]
